Somewhere around 8:30pm, I got the notification popup, which is super weird since it didn't show
up earlier and I've been running this build for half the day already. Now to figure out why!

What sucks: there's nothing at all from WearNotificationHelper in here, at all, which is
exactly where something like this *should* have appeared.

Workaround-for-now: new check for initialization before posting a notification. Since the
notification I saw had the text in it properly, then initialization necessarily already
happened, but it's at least one possible source of brian damage. Now fixed.

Meanwhile, we've got a more serious problem: the damn phantom draw-threads are back, perhaps a result
of fixing the lack of ambient mode drawing. But ambient is turned off on my watch!
